      <div class="project-meta">
       <h2 class="project-title">
        The Statistical Analysis of Your Failing Relationship
       </h2>
       <div class="project-description">
        <p>
         Ashort film that looks at our failing relationships through statistics.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          <span>
           Special Jury Award - Best Narrative Short - TriBeCa Film Festival 2015
          </span>
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>

      <div class="project-meta">
       <h2 class="project-title">
        Facebook
       </h2>
       <div class="project-description">
        <p>
         Social Film
        </p>
        <p>
         A young boy from a small town in Mexico took over the Facebook Mexico Page for 30 days page to communicate with the country and go on an unforgettable journey.
        </p>
        <p>
         Sid Lee NY
        </p>

     <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/airbnb/">
      <div class="project-meta">
       <h2 class="project-title">
        Airbnb
       </h2>
       <div class="project-description">
        <p>
         'Hollywood &amp; Vines' is the first film directed via Twitter and shot entirely on Vine by users around the world.
        </p>
        <p>
         For four days, people around the world worked with the director to share in the creation of a single story. This is the result of that global experiment, featuring 100 Viners from everywhere from Kansas to Kuwait.
        </p>
        <p>
         Mullen SF
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Branded Content Silver Pencil - The One Show 2014
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Premiered on the Sundance Channel
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

     <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/blink/">
      <div class="project-meta">
       <h2 class="project-title">
        Blink
       </h2>
       <div class="project-description">
        <p>
         Short Film
        </p>
        <p>
         An employee becomes addicted to a couple on a social network that records its users' vision with a contact lens.
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          TIFF Student Showcase - Best Live Action Film, Best Director
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Air Canada EnRoute Film Festival - Best Film, Best Director
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Montreal Film Festival - Official Selection
         </strong>
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Norman Jewison Director Award 2011
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>

     <div class="project gallery-project" data-url="/shadeofgrey/">
      <div class="project-meta">
       <h2 class="project-title">
        Shade of Grey
       </h2>
       <div class="project-description">
        <p>
         Short Documentary
        </p>
        <p>
         A portrait of the artist, Bill Beaton, in the final days of his battle with emphysema as he uses his creativity to escape the confines of a 25 ft oxygen tank tube.
        </p>
        <p>
         March 1935 - October 2009
        </p>
        <p>
         <strong>
          Best Documentary - Young Cuts Film Festival 2010
         </strong>
        </p>
       </div>
      </div>
